   BhG 13.1	Bhu 13.1
   śrī-bhagavān uvāca	SrI--BagavAn uvAca
   idaṃ śarīraṃ kaunteya kṣetram ity abhidhīyate |	idam SarIram kOnteya kzetram iti aBiDIyate |
   etad yo vetti taṃ prāhuḥ kṣetrajña iti tadvidaḥ ||1||	etat yaH vetti tam prAhuH kzetrajQaH iti tad-vidaH ||1||
   śrīdharaḥ :	SrIDaraH :
   bhaktānām aham uddhartā saṃsārād ity avādi yat |	BaktAnAm aham udDartA saMsArAt iti avAdi yat |
   tradośe 'tha tat-siddhyai tattva-jñānam udīryate ||	tradoSe aTa tat-sidDyE tattva--jQAnam udIryate ||
   teṣām ahaṃ samuddhartā mṛtyu-saṃsāra-sāgarāt, bhavāmi na cirāt pārtha	tezAm aham samudDartA mRtyu--saMsAra--sAgarAt, BavAmi na cirAt pArTa
   [Gītā 12.7] iti pūrvaṃ pratijñātam | na cātma-jñānaṃ vinā saṃsārād	[GItA 12.7] iti pUrvam pratijQAtam | na ca-Atma--jQAnam vinA saMsArAt-
   uddharaṇaṃ sambhavatīti tattva-jñānopadeśārthaṃ	udDaraNam samBavati-iti tattva--jQAna-upadeSa-arTam
   prakṛti-puruṣa-vivekādhyāya ārabhyate | tatra yat saptame 'dhyāye aparā	prakRti-puruza--viveka-aDyAyaH AraByate | tatra yat saptame aDyAye aparA
   parā ceti prakṛti-dvayam uktaṃ tayor avivekāj jīva-bhāvam āpannasya	parA ca-iti prakRti-dvayam uktam tayoH avivekAt jIva-BAvam Apannasya
   cid-aṃśasyāyaṃ saṃsāraḥ | yābhyāṃ ca jīvopabhogārtham īśvarasya	cit--aMSasya-ayam saMsAraH | yAByAm ca jIva-upaBoga-arTam ISvarasya
   sṛṣṭy-ādiṣu pravṛttiḥ | tad eva prakṛti-dvayaṃ	sRzwi--Adizu pravRttiH | tat eva prakRti-dvayam
   kṣetra-kṣetrajña-śabda-vācyaṃ parasparaṃ viviktaṃ tattvato nirūpayiṣyan	kzetra-kzetrajQa--Sabda--vAcyam parasparam viviktam tattvataH nirUpayizyan
   bhagavān uvāca idam iti | idaṃ bhogāyatanaṃ śarīraṃ kṣetram ity	BagavAn uvAca idam iti | idam Boga-Ayatanam SarIram kzetram iti-

   manyate taṃ kṣetrajña iti prāhuḥ | kṛṣībalavat tat-phala-bhoktṛtvāt |	manyate tam kzetrajQaH iti prAhuH | kRzI-bala-vat tat-Pala-BoktR-tvAt |
   tad-vidaḥ kṣetra-kṣetrajñayor vivekajñāḥ ||1||	tad--vidaH kzetra-kzetrajQayoH viveka-jQAH ||1||
   madhusūdanaḥ :	maDusUdanaH :

   jyotiḥ kiṃcana yogino yadi paraṃ paśyanti paśyantu te |	jyotiH kiMcana yoginaH yadi param paSyanti paSyantu te |

   prathama-madhyama-ṣaṭkayos tat-tvaṃ-padārthāv uktāv uttaras tu ṣaṭko	praTama-maDyama---zawkayoH tat-tvaM-pada-arTO uktO uttaraH tu zaz-kaH-
   vākyārtha-niṣṭhaḥ samyag-dhī-pradhāno 'dhunārabhyate | tatra - teṣām ahaṃ	vAkya-arTa--nizWaH samyak--DI--praDAnaH aDunA-AraByate | tatra  tezAm aham
   samuddhartā mṛtyu-saṃsāra-sāgarād bhavāmi [Gītā 12.7] iti prāg uktam | na	samudDartA mRtyu--saMsAra--sAgarAt BavAmi [GItA 12.7] iti prAk uktam | na

   vaktavyam | tac cādvitīyena paramātmanā saha jīvasyābhedam eva	vaktavyam | tat ca-advitIyena paramAtmanA saha jIvasya-aBedam eva

   vacanīyam | tad arthaṃ dehendriyāntaḥ-karaṇebhyaḥ kṣetrebhyo vivekena	vacanIyam | tat arTam deha-indriya-antaH-karaNeByaH kzetreByaH vivekena
   kṣetrajñaḥ puruṣo jīvaḥ pratikṣetram eka eva nirvikāra iti pratipādanāya	kzetrajQaH puruzaH jIvaH pratikzetram ekaH eva nirvikAraH iti pratipAdanAya
   kṣetra-kṣetrajña-vivekaḥ kriyate 'sminn adhyāye | tatra ye dve prakṛtī	kzetra-kzetrajQa--vivekaH kriyate asmin aDyAye | tatra ye dve prakRtI
   bhūmy-ādi-kṣetra-rūpatayā jīva-rūpa-kṣetrajñatayā cāpara-para-śabda-vācye	BUmi--Adi--kzetra---rUpa-tayA jIva--rUpa-kzetrajQa-tayA ca-apara--para--Sabda--vAcye

   iti |	iti |

   ity abhidhīyate | sasyasyevāsminn asakṛt karmaṇaḥ phalasya nirvṛtteḥ |	iti aBiDIyate | sasyasya-iva-asmin asakRt karmaNaH Palasya nirvRtteH |
   etad yo vetti ahaṃ mamety abhimanyate taṃ kṣetrajña iti prāhuḥ kṛṣībalavat	etat yaH vetti aham mama-iti aBimanyate tam kzetrajQaH iti prAhuH kRzI-bala-vat-

   cābhidhīyata iti karmaṇi prayogeṇa kṣetrasya jaḍatvāt karmatvaṃ	ca-aBiDIyate iti karmaNi prayogeNa kzetrasya jaxa-tvAt karma-tvam
   kṣetrajña-śabde ca dvityāṃ vinaveti-śabdam āharan svaprakāśatvāt	kzetrajQa--Sabde ca dvityAm vinaveti--Sabdam Aharan sva-prakASa-tvAt-
   karmatvābhāvam avivekina evāhuḥ sthūla-dṛśām agocaratvād iti kathayituṃ	karma-tva-aBAvam avivekinaH eva-AhuH sTUla-dRSAm agocara-tvAt iti kaTayitum

   viśvanāthaḥ :	viSvanATaH :

   niṣkāmakarma-yogināṃ bhakti-miśra-jñāṇād eva mokṣas tac ca jñānaṃ	nizkAma-karma--yoginAm Bakti-miSra--jQANAt eva mokzaH tat ca jQAnam

   BhG 13.2	Bhu 13.2
   kṣetrajñaṃ cāpi māṃ viddhi sarva-kṣetreṣu bhārata |	kzetrajQam ca-api mAm vidDi sarva-kzetrezu BArata |
   kṣetra-kṣetrajñayor jñānaṃ yat taj jñānaṃ mataṃ mama ||2||	kzetra-kzetrajQayoH jQAnam yat tat jQAnam matam mama ||2||
   śrīdharaḥ : tad evaṃ saṃsāriṇaḥ svarūpam uktam | idānīṃ tasyaiva	SrIDaraH : tat evam saMsAriNaH sva-rUpam uktam | idAnIm tasya-eva
   pāramārthikam asaṃsāri-svarūpam āha kṣetrajñam iti | ta ca kṣetrajñaṃ	pAramArTikam asaMsAri--svarUpam Aha kzetrajQam iti | te ca kzetrajQam
   saṃsāriṇaṃ jīvaṃ vastutaḥ sarva-kṣetreṣv anugataṃ mām eva viddhi | tattvam	saMsAriNam jIvam vastutas sarva-kzetrezu anugatam mAm eva vidDi | tattvam
   asi iti śrutyā lakṣitena cid-aṃśena mad-rūpasyoktatvāt ādarārtham eva	asi iti SrutyA lakzitena cit--aMSena mad---rUpasya-ukta-tvAt Adara-arTam eva
   taj-jñānaṃ stauti | kṣetra-kṣetrajñayor yad evaṃ vailakṣaṇeyan jñānaṃ tad	taj-jQAnam stOti | kzetra-kzetrajQayoH yat evam vElakzaNeyan jQAnam tat-
   eva mokṣa-hetutvān mama jñanaṃ matam | anyat tu vṛthā-pāṇḍityam |	eva mokza--hetu-tvAt mama jQanam matam | anyat tu vRTA-a--pANxityam |

   viśvanāthaḥ : adhyāyam upasaṃharati kṣetreṇa saha kṣetrajñayor	viSvanATaH : aDyAyam upasaMharati kzetreNa saha kzetrajQayoH-
   jīvātma-paramātmanor antaraṃ bhedaṃ tathā bhūtānāṃ prāṇināṃ prakṛteḥ	jIvAtma--paramAtmanoH antaram Bedam taTA BUtAnAm prANinAm prakRteH
   sakāśān mokṣaṃ mokṣopāyaṃ dhyānādikaṃ ca ye vidus te paraṃ padaṃ yānti	sakASAt mokzam mokza-upAyam DyAna-Adikam ca ye viduH te param padam yAnti
   dvayoḥ kṣetrajñayor madhye jīvātmā kṣetra-dharma-bhāk |	dvayoH kzetrajQayoH maDye jIvAtmA kzetra-Darma--BAj |
   badhyate mucyate jñānād ity adhyāyārtha īritaḥ ||	baDyate mucyate jQAnAt iti aDyAya-arTaH IritaH ||
   iti sārārtha-varṣiṇyāṃ harṣiṇyāṃ bhakta-cetasām |	iti sAra-arTa-varziNyAm harziNyAm Bakta--cetasAm |
   trayodaśo 'yaṃ gītāsu saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||	trayodaSaH ayam gItAsu saFgataH saFgataH satAm ||
   baladevaḥ : adhyāyārtham upasaṃharan taj-jñāna-phalam āha kṣetreti |	baladevaH : aDyAya-arTam upasaMharan taj-jQAna-Palam Aha kzetra-iti |
   kṣetreṇa sahitayoḥ kṣetrajñayor jīveśayor evaṃ mad-ukti-vidhayāntaraṃ	kzetreNa sahitayoH kzetrajQayoH jIveSayoH evam mad--ukti--viDayA-antaram
   bhedaṃ jñāna-cakṣuṣā vaidharmya-viṣayaka-prajñā-netreṇa ye vidus	Bedam jQAna-cakzuzA vEDarmya--vizaya-ka-prajQA--netreNa ye viduH-
   tathābhūtānāṃ prakṛteḥ sakāśān mokṣaṃ ca tat-sādhanam amānitvādikaṃ ye	taTABUtAnAm prakRteH sakASAt mokzam ca tat--sADanam amAni-tva-Adikam ye
   vidus te prakṛteḥ paraṃ sarvotkṛṣṭaṃ para-vyomākhyaṃ mat-padaṃ yāntīti	viduH te prakRteH param sarva-utkRzwam para-vyoma-AKyam mat--padam yAnti-iti
   jīveśau deha-madhyasthau tatrādyo deha-dharma-yuk |	jIveSO deha--maDya-sTO tatra-AdyaH deha--Darma--yuj |
   badhyate mucyate bodhād iti jñānaṃ trayodaśāt ||	baDyate mucyate boDAt iti jQAnam trayodaSAt ||
   iti śrīmad-bhagavad-gītopaniṣad-bhāṣye trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||13||	iti SrI-mat--Bagavat--gIta-upanizad--BAzye trayodaSaH aDyAyaH ||13||
   [*ENDNOTE] All the verses quoted here are found in Rāmānuja 's commentary.	[*ENDNOTE] Alt Te verseH quotet here are fount id RAmAnuja as ca-ummentary.
   bhagavad-gītā - trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ	Bagavat--gItAH  trayodaSaH aDyAyaH
